2.1.1  container rw-redundancy:redundancy-config
  Description
    RIFT.ware redundancy configuration node.
  Leaves
    name: dns-ip-fqdn, type: UNION, description: The IP address or the domain name to use which
    the DNS would resolve to the ACTIVE site.
    name: preferred-site, type: STRING, description: Preferred site name.
  XPath Path
    /rw-redundancy:redundancy-config
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-redundancy:redundancy-config

2.1.1.1  list rw-redundancy:site
  Description
    The list of sites to be configured for
    redundancy.
  Leaves
    name: site-name, type: STRING, description: The name of the redunduncy site.

  XPath Path

2.1.1.1.1  list rw-redundancy:rw-instances
  Description
    List of RIFT.ware instances running
    under a site. The number of RIFT.ware
    instances under a site depends upon the
    redundancy model.
  Leaves
    name: rwinstance-id, type: STRING, description: The unique name assigned to the riftware instance.
    Should be what RW environment variable RW_SYSTEM_NAME is set to.
    name: floating-ip, type: UNION, description: The IP address associated with the floating
    point interface
  XPath Path
    /rw-redundancy:redundancy-config/rw-redundancy:site/rw-redundancy:rw-instances
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-redundancy:redundancy-config/rw-redundancy:site[rw-redundancy:site-name='STRING']/rw-redundancy:rw-instances[rw-redundancy:rwinstance-id='STRING']
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-redundancy:redundancy-config/site/STRING/rw-instances/STRING
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    C,/rw-redundancy:redundancy-config/rw-redundancy:site/rw-redundancy:rw-instances
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    C,/rw-redundancy:redundancy-config/rw-redundancy:site[rw-redundancy:site-name='STRING']/rw-redundancy:rw-instances[rw-redundancy:rwinstance-id='STRING']
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_redundancy.YangData.RwRedundancy.RedundancyConfig.Site.RwInstances

2.1.1.2  container rw-redundancy:polling-config
  Description
    Settings for polling status of the peer
    RIFT.ware instance. To be used by the service
    which determines the status and elects the RIFT.ware
    instance as ACTIVE or STANDBY.
  Leaves
    name: poll-interval, type: UINT32, description: Interval for polling status.
    name: full-state-resync-time, type: UINT32, description: Time interval after which full state(config + package)
    resync would be performed.
    Resync is always initiated by the STANDBY.
    name: config-push-bulk-wait-time, type: UINT32, description: Time to wait to gather and batch additional
    config changes before pushing it to STANDBY.
    Zero value means for every configuration change detcted
    a package push would be initiated.
    name: mano-package-sync-wait-timeo, type: UINT32, description: Time to wait for MANO to finish package
    updation before pushing the artifacts to STANDBY
    name: election-timeo, type: UINT32, description: The duration for which the election process will run
    when the node is booted up.
    For DIRECT mode only.
    name: tie-break-timeo, type: UINT32, description: The time after which tie breaker tried to resolve active-stanby selection.
    This is run only in case of network failure
    name: config-load-timeo, type: UINT32, description: The time to wait for configuration to be loaded.
    This can be either in ACTIVE load or STANDBY takeover
    name: no-response-counter, type: UINT32, description: This counter together with poll-interval will
    determine how long to wait for the peer instance
    which is in state NO_RESPONSE to be declared DEAD.
    name: split-brain-resolution-timeo, type: UINT32, description: Time to wait to make sure both the nodes have reached
    the same state before resolving split brain conflict.
    name: failover-hysteresis-counter, type: UINT32, description: This counter together with poll-interval will
    determine how long to wait for performing failover
    when the DNS responds with IP addresses of both ACTIVE
    and STANDBY sites. For INDIRECT mode only.
  XPath Path
    /rw-redundancy:redundancy-config/rw-redundancy:polling-config
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-redundancy:redundancy-config/rw-redundancy:polling-config
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-redundancy:redundancy-config/polling-config
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    C,/rw-redundancy:redundancy-config/rw-redundancy:polling-config
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    C,/rw-redundancy:redundancy-config/rw-redundancy:polling-config
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_redundancy.YangData.RwRedundancy.RedundancyConfig.PollingConfig
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwRedundancyYang.YangData_RwRedundancy_RedundancyConfig_PollingConfig
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwRedundancy__YangData__RwRedundancy__RedundancyConfig__PollingConfig
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_data_RedundancyConfig_PollingConfig
    RwRedundancy_data_RedundancyConfig_PollingConfig
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_data_RedundancyConfig_PollingConfig

2.1.2.1  container rw-redundancy:active-instance
  Description
    Details of the active RIFT.ware instance.
  Leaves
    name: active-inst-id, type: UNION
    name: site-name, type: STRING, description: Name of the site where active is running.
    name: is-this-instance-active, type: BOOLEAN, description: Set to true if this RIFT.ware instance is the active
    one or not.
  XPath Path
    /rw-redundancy:redundancy-state/rw-redundancy:active-instance
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-redundancy:redundancy-state/rw-redundancy:active-instance
  RW.REST URI Path

2.4.8.1.3  container rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-state-bug/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-state-bug/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-state-bug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:gr-state-bug/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:gr-state-bug/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_redundancy.YangNotif.RwRedundancy.GrStateBug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwRedundancyYang.YangNotif_RwRedundancy_GrStateBug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwRedundancy__YangNotif__RwRedundancy__GrStateBug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_GrStateBug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwRedundancy_notif_GrStateBug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_GrStateBug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.4.9.1.3  container rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-state-debug/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-state-debug/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-state-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:gr-state-debug/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:gr-state-debug/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_redundancy.YangNotif.RwRedundancy.GrStateDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwRedundancyYang.YangNotif_RwRedundancy_GrStateDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwRedundancy__YangNotif__RwRedundancy__GrStateDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_GrStateDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwRedundancy_notif_GrStateDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_GrStateDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.4.11.1.3  container rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-state-notice/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-state-notice/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-state-notice/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:gr-state-notice/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:gr-state-notice/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_redundancy.YangNotif.RwRedundancy.GrStateNotice.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwRedundancyYang.YangNotif_RwRedundancy_GrStateNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwRedundancy__YangNotif__RwRedundancy__GrStateNotice__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_GrStateNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

  YPBC Base Identifier

2.4.14.1.3  container rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-package-info/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-package-info/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-package-info/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:gr-package-info/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:gr-package-info/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_redundancy.YangNotif.RwRedundancy.GrPackageInfo.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwRedundancyYang.YangNotif_RwRedundancy_GrPackageInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwRedundancy__YangNotif__RwRedundancy__GrPackageInfo__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_GrPackageInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwRedundancy_notif_GrPackageInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_GrPackageInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.4.16.1.3  container rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-package-warning/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-package-warning/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-package-warning/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:gr-package-warning/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:gr-package-warning/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_redundancy.YangNotif.RwRedundancy.GrPackageWarning.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwRedundancyYang.YangNotif_RwRedundancy_GrPackageWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwRedundancy__YangNotif__RwRedundancy__GrPackageWarning__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_GrPackageWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwRedundancy_notif_GrPackageWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_GrPackageWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.4.19.1.3  container rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-redundancy:standby-action-info/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-redundancy:standby-action-info/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-redundancy:standby-action-info/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:standby-action-info/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:standby-action-info/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_redundancy.YangNotif.RwRedundancy.StandbyActionInfo.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwRedundancyYang.YangNotif_RwRedundancy_StandbyActionInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwRedundancy__YangNotif__RwRedundancy__StandbyActionInfo__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_StandbyActionInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwRedundancy_notif_StandbyActionInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_StandbyActionInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.4.21.1.3  container rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-redundancy:active-action-debug/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-redundancy:active-action-debug/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-redundancy:active-action-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:active-action-debug/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:active-action-debug/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_redundancy.YangNotif.RwRedundancy.ActiveActionDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwRedundancyYang.YangNotif_RwRedundancy_ActiveActionDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwRedundancy__YangNotif__RwRedundancy__ActiveActionDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_ActiveActionDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwRedundancy_notif_ActiveActionDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_ActiveActionDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_ActiveActionNotice_TemplateParams_AdditionalData

2.4.23.1.3  container rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-redundancy:active-action-notice/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-redundancy:active-action-notice/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-redundancy:active-action-notice/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:active-action-notice/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:active-action-notice/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_redundancy.YangNotif.RwRedundancy.ActiveActionNotice.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwRedundancyYang.YangNotif_RwRedundancy_ActiveActionNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwRedundancy__YangNotif__RwRedundancy__ActiveActionNotice__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_ActiveActionNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwRedundancy_notif_ActiveActionNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_ActiveActionNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.4.26.1.3  container rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-app-notice/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-app-notice/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-app-notice/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:gr-app-notice/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:gr-app-notice/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_redundancy.YangNotif.RwRedundancy.GrAppNotice.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwRedundancyYang.YangNotif_RwRedundancy_GrAppNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwRedundancy__YangNotif__RwRedundancy__GrAppNotice__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_GrAppNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwRedundancy_notif_GrAppNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_GrAppNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-election-debug/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-election-debug/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-election-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:gr-election-debug/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:gr-election-debug/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_redundancy.YangNotif.RwRedundancy.GrElectionDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwRedundancyYang.YangNotif_RwRedundancy_GrElectionDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.4.29.1.3  container rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-election-info/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-election-info/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-election-info/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:gr-election-info/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:gr-election-info/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_redundancy.YangNotif.RwRedundancy.GrElectionInfo.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier

    RwRedundancyYang.YangNotif_RwRedundancy_GrElectionInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.4.31.1.3  container rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-tie-break-debug/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-tie-break-debug/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-tie-break-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:gr-tie-break-debug/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:gr-tie-break-debug/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_redundancy.YangNotif.RwRedundancy.GrTieBreakDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwRedundancyYang.YangNotif_RwRedundancy_GrTieBreakDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwRedundancy__YangNotif__RwRedundancy__GrTieBreakDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_GrTieBreakDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwRedundancy_notif_GrTieBreakDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_GrTieBreakDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

    rw_ypbc_RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_GrTieBreakNotice_TemplateParams_AdditionalData

2.4.33.1.3  container rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-tie-break-notice/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-tie-break-notice/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-tie-break-notice/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:gr-tie-break-notice/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:gr-tie-break-notice/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_redundancy.YangNotif.RwRedundancy.GrTieBreakNotice.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwRedundancyYang.YangNotif_RwRedundancy_GrTieBreakNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwRedundancy__YangNotif__RwRedundancy__GrTieBreakNotice__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_GrTieBreakNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwRedundancy_notif_GrTieBreakNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier

2.4.36.1.3  container rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-split-brain-notice/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-split-brain-notice/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-redundancy:gr-split-brain-notice/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:gr-split-brain-notice/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-redundancy:gr-split-brain-notice/rw-redundancy:template_params/rw-redundancy:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_redundancy.YangNotif.RwRedundancy.GrSplitBrainNotice.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwRedundancyYang.YangNotif_RwRedundancy_GrSplitBrainNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwRedundancy__YangNotif__RwRedundancy__GrSplitBrainNotice__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_GrSplitBrainNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwRedundancy_notif_GrSplitBrainNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwRedundancy_RwRedundancy_notif_GrSplitBrainNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
